< review>
Excessive damage to rims with installation of tires.  Replaced 2 tires and work done was unprofessional.  Paint on rims was freshly chipped and peeling.  Edge of rims were freshly damaged and shards of aluminum were freshly ground and splintering.  The damage was all new and the chips and shards were splintered and able to be removed with my finger verifying the damage was new.  Rims are 14 years old, discontinued and irreplaceable Lincoln OEM.  Not the first replacement of tires and not curb damage.  No such edge damage on other 2 rims verifying the work had been done numerous times previously without damage and able to be done professionally.  Also, it took 2 hours to work on and damage 2 tires.  I'm going to ask for a refund on installation, all the warranty/balance and hazard coverage.  Went there so I could use my Sears Credit card with 12 month payments and cause I use Craftsman tools.  Never going there again.  Googled Sears Tire complaints and first one I read was the same exact situation/damage on $2000 Mercedes rims.</review>

Current review 2018,;

Well I have reviewed this place more then once,
And time around is a different story, it's not the same quality service that it once was.
Old review: 2016 ; What can I say, $14.99 oil changes plus $7.99 filter and you can make an online appointment it's perfect!!

If you don't have an appointment the wait time sucks, when they're working on your car a text message is sent to your phone if they find other problems with your car? so unless you reply to the text messages they hold your car until they've spoken to you. if there's a fan belt that needs to be replaced I guess that's a good thing? but it just depends if they want to change something that doesn't need to be replaced which was the case in my experience.

**On the plus side, When you get an oil change here, they do a "Pro Snap Shot" of you car,  this means they profile your car, i.e  tires, battery, alignment, transmission  oil level, computer scan and tire pressure. Every time I'm here they say "Battery Unreachable" "Transmission Oil Unreachable"? Ok, guys,  My Battery is in the trunk? it's a Jaguar and easy to find. My "Transmission oil level is located at the bottom of my car near the Motor Oil Pan" very close to where they drain my oil from?.  Something not right here?

There's two guys who's very nice "Mike" "William" the girls are not really nice. And assistant Manager is William.. I believe The actual manager is a female but I don't know her name.

A regular turnaround time for a  oil change here  is 1 hour, if you think that's too long then don't come here... But  if you think that's OK then by all means you found yourself a fordable/quality place to do your future oil changes.

General labor costs are high here at $90 per hour. I asked them to do my eight spark plugs for me and they wanted to charge me about $150 just for labor and another $90 for parts.

I was also told they do AC service here: I will keep you guys posted....

*Recap: 3 months later...*Continuation from last post: I did have my AC service here and everything turned out great! They found that it was only a small peace needed replacement and it was only couple of dollars to replace, in actuality  the whole thing cost me about $130-$150 and I believe that's reasonable.

They  also have basic maintenance services available, such as: transmission maintenance, radiator flush, spark plug replacement, hit night restoration, cabin and intake air filter replacement and much more.< /text>

< review>
Hard gravel 4-5ft in width. Wheelchair accessible with, I think it was 3 or 4 handicapped parking spots. Accessible outhouse style toilets with a concrete floor and raised oval toilets and plenty of TP. Accessed on Walker Rd off of Hwy 199 near Crescent City, CA. Very worth it. Old growth Redwoods, creek with accessible bridges. Free. My favorite. I live in Brookings and come here regularly. Best to come when the sun is high.<//review>

This is the BEST vet in the Temecula Valley!! We first went to them a year ago with a sick class guinea pig who sadly passed while we were there to see if we could save her. The staff was INCREDIBLY nurturing and helpful in allowing us to process it all (my children were with me). They even sent a sorrow card after our visit to check on us and make sure we were ok. From that point I knew this was our vet!

Fast forward a year later, we have 2 of our own guinea pigs, and one of them appeared to have the beginning of an eye infection. We are in the middle of this "stay home" quarantine but I knew this needed to be addressed as soon as possible. Called CARE and they got us an appointment the next day, AND following all state guidelines to remain at safe distances, they have their office closed and have staff come to the car to take pets in so there is no waiting room/possibility of being in close proximity with other patient's parents. < Text>
I found a medium size parrot, and noticed it scratching a lot, and loosing a large amount of feathers on a daily basis. In researching online, I concluded it had bird mites and proceeded to look for a bird veterinarian. I came across this facility, and made an appointment. The office was a little tricky to find, but upon arrival it appeared clean and kept up. My review is mostly based on  their rates. I was assisted initially by the vet assistant, friendly, nice, and then by the young veterinarian gentleman, also very friendly and nice, and spent a good amount of time with me and my bird, and offered good follow up advice. I brought in a bag of a red mite I had caught on my bird's cage, but it either got out by the time I arrived, as we could not find it in the bag to confirm my bird had mites. I felt I had to really convince the assistant & Doctor that the bird had mites, as they really didn't do anything in the examination to confirm why the bird was itching & losing so many feathers. My dissatisfaction comes from not understanding how they can charge such high fees for first, the initial examination of $45.60, then a recommended beak, nail, and wing trim @ $88.35, and 1 of 3 scheduled injections for mites @ $53.68 each!! Grand total, first visit=$187.63! This is a bird! Not the size of a dog,  or a cat, and yet the fees are this high! This is the main reason people DO NOT take their pets to the Vet when the pet clearly needs medical attention! Pets suffer due to these high vet fees, as the normal person does not have these kind of funds to spend, even though they truly desire to help their pets feel better. Now, the big push is for recommending pet insurance, which they like clock work, sent me in the mail. This way the Vets can continue increasing their fees, knowing the insurance the Customer has will pay out. It's just like regular Health Insurance for people, a total Scam!   I want my bird to get better, and therefore I am committed to finish the next 2 rounds of injections that they recommended @ $53.68 each, more.  And F.Y.I. to Staff there, we, the Clients, can hear everything you are talking about while we are waiting for the doctor in those rooms. I would suggest you keep your private conversations about your love life relationships, just that, private, and to be discussed during non business, or lunch time hours.< /Text>

<name>Cali Girl in WV</name><Time>1528213270827< /Time><Rating>5</Rating>< review>
Dr. Alcorn has been treating our exotic pet for almost four years. We found him completely by chance while looking for someone who would treat exotics in the area. I couldnt be happier that we found him. Our pet was suddenly ill and losing hair and losing weight. Dr Alcorn was so kind and thorough and found that our little guy had adrenal disease and insulinoma. He took plenty of time explaining everything to us and helping us understand why our seemingly healthy pet was suddenly tanking and what could be done. The prognosis wasn't great but managable for a time. Under Dr. Alcorn's care our little guy has lived much longer than expected. Dr. Alcorn is always kind, patient with our questions, gives a thorough explanation of what is happening, and has a great bedside manner with our pet.
Don't let me forget the staff, who are wonderful! They always call to check on our little guy and see how he's doing. I have to call there regularly to get medication refills and they are always very pokite and helpful and get it taken care of quickly, and they never fail to ask how he is doing while they have me on the phone. I can't express enough how appreciative I am of the entire staff. I would recommend this office to anyone looking for a great vet!!!</review>

< Review>

The source for those funds come from ALL taxpayers and not just those who this center tends to ‚Äúfavor‚Äù in providing services.  They do not serve just the Hispanics or Filipino population but a large number of Blacks utilize this facility as well; and it‚Äôs this particular group of individuals that this center elects - openly - to overlook.  Limited programming (unlike that given to either LGBTQ or women).  A lack of Black staff.  But a disproportionate number of DOS in correlation to others I‚Äôve personally speak up to have the voice heard as it relates to services. <user_id>103814051022694015744< /user_id>< Text>
If you are homeless, this is one of the two places to visit ASAP, the other is 1235 Mission Street where the office for San Francisco's Human Services is located.

Most people direct the homeless to the MSC or Multi Services Center, which happens to have all the desirable services. Except the Security Guards treat everyone that comes in as if they were a dangerous guilty convicted felon, no exceptions. Partly because of their paranoid attitude and poor understanding of other cultures (racism biases, stereotypes,  and limited english) Unless you were a known celebrity or city official, then they either behave or hide out of sight.
At the MNRC or Mission Neighborhood Resource Center, they treat everyone with genuine honesty, dignity and human courtesy. Not like a convict.
There is also a clinic on site Mon thru Fri, for medical service and referrals for specialist needs. Unlike MSC there is a patio on the 2nd floor for smokers.
Unfortunately the facility is limited due to its small building. If they had more donors and donations they could offer more services and help people better.

Right now it is limited to a maximum of 75 persons at any given time, during normal business hours.

To be processed in order to participate and get on the waiting lists for shelters, and single night emergency shelter.
You will have to come by early in the morning, once you've been processed into the DHSA's computer system. M - F to get signed into the days eligibility list for one night emergency shelter stays. Before normal opening hours, usually around 5 am, for the shower list, shelter list, and the laundry waiting list for the day.
Sometimes the line starts sooner, like 4 or 3 am, from time to time.
On cold wet rainy days, the line is usually smaller and later. Bring an umbrella, there is no awnings for 99.2% of the buildings in this city.< /Text>

Fish and topping choices are similar to most other poke shops, but I like how this place lets you mix and match different types of sauces!
The first scoop of massage, crab meat, and avocado are free which is always a plus :)
My friend and I placed an order online for pick up and was ready when we got there.
All staff were wearing masks with glass screen near the register, +1 for taking Covid precautions!

The seafood tasted fresh with an generous amount of toppings.
It was a little hard to mix due to the copious amount of toppings but other than that amazing!

<time>1595370735706<//time><rate>4< /rate>< review>
Honestly unsure why this place receives such high reviews. As a poke junkie, this place to me was very basic.

Wasn't impressed with the crab salad, and the rice was cold. They don't mix in the traditional mix ins with the sauce, and the mix in options were thin.

Overall the options were decent, prices were fair, but definitely wasn't the best or worst poke place I've been to. The guy who served me got my order wrong twice (probably because of speaking through plexi glass and a mask)

Nice location that offers outdoor seating, stopped here while shopping.</review>
